Issue #20788: Labels: bug, pending, en

Issue #20781: Labels: not-related, en, third-party
Use shallow API for any complex third-party instance object.\n\n```diff\n- const myChart = ref(null);\n+ const myChart = shallowRef(null);\n```\n\nOr change the `myChart` ref to a local variable.\n\nSee also [FAQ](https://echarts.apache.org/faq.html#others).

Issue #20726: Labels: bug, pending, en
As per [documentation](https://echarts.apache.org/en/option.html#xAxis.minorTick.splitNumber) `minorTick.splitNumber` revers to the number of **intervals**, not the number of minorTicks / splitLines.  The documentation does not specify what exactly is split tho. It seems to be the interval between two labels (which is not neccessarily equal to the interval between two ticks).\n\nIf you align ticks and axisLabel it should work as expected: [Example](https://echarts.apache.org/examples/en/editor.html?c=line-simple&code=MYewdgzgLgBANgUzDAvDAjABkwbgFCiSwAeAIgIZTmowCCATveQJ4B0AZvSALYAUA3vCQBzKAAsAXEOQBfADQxeASlQA-PDBgBZSmI5wQIerx3jWTMABMeymACppSvEvyFoMZhSo0GTNpxtBRDBRSWkYeUUANwUAaxUUVRhYmABqDBcCcHdLSmo0TzzWbnIAB15eRHYoBQBLS2IEpIBtKpqYMjzm-uIAXV7MvBBSqFrwGn4NDtpiWogpSc1NKGZShCkAcijyOABXBA25Kc1yWYgAFVrgWIXjpZ3a4TAAdVrxABlyACMEOCkoej7I5LCLApYQUpwN7vWpgdYwRYgmAQMQgADu_0BCDBIKhcIAyitEAsYKADPRNvQEJYNhE7vI7txYUZLtdbkjkaiMTAAUC7poIVCoAA5XbcH4UmAANnpOJgTLARnxkOhsPhiJBKPRmL5HLxCEJzGJCNJIHJm2EVKQtJksqmDM0zBmcwWDuRCHotQQ8xgzTuGqWKzWm31h35yOY4rNm0VcLDHNyVCkifI9KmvTwMhwQA)\n\nIf you need specific tick intervals you can control them with [interval](https://echarts.apache.org/en/option.html#xAxis.interval), [minInterval ](https://echarts.apache.org/en/option.html#xAxis.minInterval) and [maxInterval](https://echarts.apache.org/en/option.html#xAxis.maxInterval): [Example](https://echarts.apache.org/examples/en/editor.html?c=line-simple&code=MYewdgzgLgBANgUzDAvDAjABkwbgFCiSwAeAIgIZTmowCCATveQJ4B0AZvSALYAUA3vCQBzKAAsAXEOQBfADQxeASlQA-PDBgBZSmI5wQIerx3jWTMABMeymACppSvEvyFoMZhSo0GTNpxtBRDBRSWkYeUUANwUAaxUUVRhYmABqDBcCcHdLSmo0TzzWbnIAB15eRHYoBQBLS2IEpIBtKpqYMjzm-uIAXV7MvBBSqFrwGn4NDtpiWogpSc1NKGZShCkAcijyOABXBA25Kc1asCgEem24KQBWI6WYclmIABVa4FiF46Wd2uEwADqtXEABlyAAjBDXGBQej7e5LeTfCClODAkGndYwRYPGAQMQgADuUlh8O-mjRYAQAGUVogFjBQAZ6Jt6AhLBsIt8kQ9uKcjG8Pl9cXiCcSYXCEAiHii0VAAHK7biQlkwABs3OlMD5YCM1NR6Mxwtx-KJJMlWopmNpzHp2MZIGZm2EbKQnJkmqmPI8MzmC29EAutQQ8xgzW-OIeKzWm0pB0teOYysdm11VMO5JguSoUmz5G5U16eBkOCAA)

Issue #20655: Labels: bug, pending, en
This only happens if you move a node out of the initially rendered axis range because the visible nodes and the invisible graphics elements are no longer aligned. When the axis range changes, the nodes are rerendered to their new pixel position (coordinate position stays the the same) while the pixel position of  the invisible graphics elements doesnt change.\r\n\r\nIf you set `invisable: false` you can oberve what is happening.

Issue #20629: Labels: bug, pending, missing-demo, waiting-for: author

Issue #20628: Labels: bug, pending, en
I do not think this is a bug. Two series in a **single** chart have a **single** tooltip activated on _mousemove_ by default.\r\nEvent _mousemove_ has precedence over action _showTip_. So once a tooltip is activated in one series, _showTip_ will not work in the other because only one tooltip is allowed.

Issue #20616: Labels: bug, pending, en

Issue #20575: Labels: new-feature, en, wontfix
That being said, you could still provide a width calculated from some parameters you know. For example, if we know the inner radius `r0` and outer radius `r1` of a certain level, and you have `n` nodes of this level, then we know that the tangential text width can be approximated to around `2 * Math.PI * (r0 / 2 + r1 / 2) / n`.

Issue #20526: Labels: bug, pending, en
not-a-bug, _visualMap.selected_ is not included in chart configuration option API. \r\nBut it could be set by action [selectDataRange](https://echarts.apache.org/en/api.html#action.visualMap.selectDataRange). Dispatch this action after your _myChart.setOption_ call.\r\nüìå please close issue if problem solved.

Issue #20520: Labels: support, SSR
Line chart have default animation in symbol and label. \r\n\r\nSSR with canvas render not support animation.  disable it, the image will be right.\r\n\r\nTry `animation: false`.\r\n\r\nAll options are below\r\n\r\n```js\r\n{\r\n  title: {\r\n    text: "10.01-10.15Êó•Ê¥ªÊØèÊó•Â¢ûÈïøË∂ãÂäø",\r\n  },\r\n  animation: false,\r\n  tooltip: {},\r\n  legend: {\r\n    data: ["Ê¥ªË∑ÉÊï∞"],\r\n    bottom: "10",\r\n  },\r\n  xAxis: {\r\n    data: [\r\n      "2024-10-1",\r\n      "2024-10-2",\r\n      "2024-10-3",\r\n      "2024-10-4",\r\n      "2024-10-5",\r\n      "2024-10-6",\r\n      "2024-10-7",\r\n      "2024-10-8",\r\n      "2024-10-9",\r\n      "2024-10-10",\r\n      "2024-10-11",\r\n      "2024-10-12",\r\n      "2024-10-13",\r\n      "2024-10-14",\r\n      "2024-10-15",\r\n    ],\r\n  },\r\n  yAxis: {},\r\n  series: [\r\n    {\r\n      name: "Ê¥ªË∑ÉÊï∞",\r\n      type: "line",\r\n      data: [\r\n        86, 38, 45, 37, 37, 37, 60, 589, 545, 653, 891, 838, 225, 708, 597,\r\n      ],\r\n      label: {\r\n        show: true, // ÊòæÁ§∫ÊØè‰∏™Êï∞ÊçÆÁÇπÁöÑÊ†áÁ≠æ\r\n        position: "top", // Ê†áÁ≠æÁöÑ‰ΩçÁΩÆÔºåÂèØ‰ª•ÊòØ \

Issue #20512: Labels: bug, pending, en

Issue #20416: Labels: en, not-a-bug
This is not a bug.\r\n\r\nPlease read the [doc](https://echarts.apache.org/zh/api.html#echartsInstance.setOption) carefully.\r\n\r\nWhen using replace merge, series is merged based on id. So when you calling `setOption` for the second time, labelLayout is not provided and thus the old labelLayout is used (merged).\r\n\r\nTo fully reset the series, you need to set a different `series.id` the second time you calling `setOption`, or you can set `notMerge` to be `true` to force not using merging.

Issue #20412: Labels: bug, pending, en
_boundingCoords_ are not well explained in API. In addition of zooming to a predefined area, they also limit the mouse interaction with the map. Pan/zoom are **disabled** outside the rectangular boundary.\r\nUse _geo.center_ and _geo.zoom_ instead of _geo.boundingCoords_ if you want to pan/zoom over the entire map.\r\n[Demo](https://echarts.apache.org/examples/en/editor.html?c=map-usa-pie&code=PTAEBUAsEsGdQKYA8CGBbADgGwaATggI4Cu0B8AogMKQp4Au8AbgKwB0ALGwAygD2eUFhT0EeAFBYsSUAF5QAWgAc7AGwslAZlWaA3EKwBPOaE0B2NgE5NAJi2rd44nhnzlXc2bOaAjPufGsgCQmpZsPiw2ZhwsjgBGfMQAdgAm0EkA5lR8Aimw8gDaoAVSSAA0BoYAuhUFzuVBAVWgVY5ohjR09GywkHwA7gAyfChpmQAUAJSOACRsGQj04wBKAPKr4AD6AAoAguAAEqAA1KAA5MApIijAKLCwi8ALfMAAqgDKu2wAVrB8SWcKgAzZIAY3o0H-oHGxFgKAAUn8kpNQABvcSgRCg2gMWBsAgZOCiPAAWRQGHGZw-u0BoFhCKRFXRmMxu2EsAA1igAFxojEszE4IH0XkKHy-Mr8gX0PgYXk2FiSgWY_rQFL0SC8iJS0AAXyVLIOKH6KGg0F5zOVQpFih8Pm4BulsvlSkdLNV6s1oBYOv1OrO22IYhloGW0FBfDOFp1goQwtFZlUbsxMrloBsSZjoA9Gvlvv5uum_JBSXBkKS-BQqT4aG20AQ7zE9dg41BCCSxIqeFG0FhKMtmIjSVg9FAV3oKBMBTONIqZwAQrSzlQlwARM5VNhocnjcb0FGyAB8fOV-EWzgrA-VTBQWCDvLJGvxiVS40fkHxVZSNamoAAVKA9rcJMyYskk6AILyy4iAgGQCMYZwnKA9BZrqjgCoW6EsgQ9AXieyr0IYGCQecGD1oCWYRrk6Qwe8hgjggaBQc8FGnjKfBYBCaZXgKQICNu9DElBqJxLqFqgrq0KoikuoAKSTGcqGgcIcQIFg0anpivQDLyQK3g8SlZipamDOkJE8Sy2n9Lp-kIIZp5VtAAnlquzgiOWvIOlm3ZpLCoFth2YigeOKC-lhur8rKEJQvIV7PBpyrbmmVKfKxyp4CMTHIXgQagSAAVCcUyjsNwPhKNwiqmEobAsBwUSWDUoAAF45FlZWgQkyRjFkOR4HkvpuuxnHQNxfoCjgCypBaY2WU2CCwLyBRZqiyFESRZxYGZsC0hgHGGJtSSQfQOUIBUWaYiF3IFCtVF9QtS2aSyJTSGUQRSNUtSlK9TRnY9mJ1C4ZQBEEjUA-UlSg19b1GM0zS6jU9npV-NZ1g2c0tgUxU8GVFUVJo1W1fVjURCB3nI7W9aNngzbjJjdqqGwKiaCw3AcHjYRKI1CqkwKVQFlh7SdAwbAwCkCDDD2ExFpigs4t0Dz0KsGDRUk4xReWRaYUAA)\r\n\r\n![image](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/02f79c62-f1ad-4436-b2db-50fc85e2a270)\r\nüìå please close issue if problem solved.

Issue #20403: Labels: bug, pending, en
The properties [zlevel](https://echarts.apache.org/en/option.html#series-line.zlevel) and [z](https://echarts.apache.org/en/option.html#series-line.z) only exist on series level, not on markArea level. The z value of the markArea seems to be hard coded and unrelated to the z value of the containing series.\r\n\r\nMarkLine seems to have a higher z value and can be used as an alternative in your case: [Example](https://echarts.apache.org/examples/en/editor.html?code=PYBwLglsB2AEC8sDeAoWsAeBBDEDOAXMmurGAJ4gCmRA5JALZW0kC-ANCeTvkaqWUo1YtAG4BDADYBXZm07o8VAE4QqhWAG0S6fgNjRxTOgGUVavLACMtBforU6kiNGZ2BAE3FhxRbftJNWgAmAAZggBYAWlCrGJt2WDCAXXd9ILDI-Jjg21gAVlDUnXSQ8OjYmIBmPKsUtIEM8uzQiLyADiKS9GKAgC8iKxKOEr0BQ2MRM1V1JNtuwUcRZ1d5gK8fPwX0JqzK2NrQoobAsr248NrO3oCtM4qLmsSANmPtu8yHmLbEqyqugI3AQDazDNJjUgTYS0ACy4mUAGtYFhlFRxGt7EInC43AsNr4tEDSAx4QiUWi-O98VtboF3gIIbT0NxcBpCvTSCMmaRGUyWbxrOzuehWBzku8icCiKETugIGAqAwTBRJMJeQIAMbASTAZR0ZQAcwARuIABTBfL5X4AdiqNutiVCADoIgBKFi00UBL2c8ELKF0OGI2AAGRxGIEDmhK1x628BM0ktgJMRYdclNp1K0HKQ_LZoR9gNlsBjyvIqozTNA4g18vIg2L6CjdDw2ogHgjty1Or1IlRHcbsAA7u2wAALIj5d5c254cgMI3aujQGCx26ScRGqiSPh4MfAIdEABmUiUhc5wxI4tYAG4gA)
